\newcommand*\pandocbounded[1]{% scales image to fit in text height/width
  \sbox\pandoc@box{#1}%
  \Gscale@div\@tempa{\textheight}{\dimexpr\ht\pandoc@box+\dp\pandoc@box\relax}%
  \Gscale@div\@tempb{\linewidth}{\wd\pandoc@box}%
  \ifdim\@tempb\p@<\@tempa\p@\let\@tempa\@tempb\fi% select the smaller of both
  \ifdim\@tempa\p@<\p@\scalebox{\@tempa}{\usebox\pandoc@box}%
  \else\usebox{\pandoc@box}%
  \fi%
}

\begin{tcolorbox}[enhanced jigsaw, bottomtitle=1mm, titlerule=0mm, arc=.35mm, colback=white, title=\textcolor{quarto-callout-tip-color}{\faLightbulb}\hspace{0.5em}{æç¤º}, coltitle=black, leftrule=.75mm, opacityback=0, colbacktitle=quarto-callout-tip-color!10!white, toprule=.15mm, opacitybacktitle=0.6, colframe=quarto-callout-tip-color-frame, toptitle=1mm, rightrule=.15mm, breakable, left=2mm, bottomrule=.15mm]

\begin{enumerate}
\def\labelenumi{\arabic{enumi}.}

\section{å›žå½’ä»»åŠ¡ï¼ˆRegressionï¼‰}\label{ux56deux5f52ux4efbux52a1regression}

\section{çº¿æ€§æ¨¡åž‹ä¸­çš„æ­£åˆ™åŒ–}\label{ux7ebfux6027ux6a21ux578bux4e2dux7684ux6b63ux5219ux5316}

\subsection{1. å²­å›žå½’ï¼ˆRidge

\section{å›žå½’ä»»åŠ¡æŒ‡æ ‡}\label{ux56deux5f52ux4efbux52a1ux6307ux6807}

  RMSE ä¸Ž \(y\) åŒé‡çº²ï¼Œæ›´æ˜“è§£é‡Š

\subsection{2.

\begin{itemize}
\tightlist
\item
  å¯¹å¼‚å¸¸å€¼æ›´é²æ£’
\end{itemize}

\subsection{\texorpdfstring{3.
å†³å®šç³»æ•°ï¼ˆ\(R^2\)ï¼‰}{3. å†³å®šç³»æ•°ï¼ˆR\^{}2ï¼‰}}\label{ux51b3ux5b9aux7cfbux6570r2}

\[

\begin{itemize}
\tightlist

  è¡¡é‡æ¨¡åž‹è§£é‡Šçš„æ–¹å·®æ¯”ä¾‹
\item
  æ ·æœ¬å†… \(R^2\) æ€»æ˜¯ \(\leq 1\)

\subsection{\texorpdfstring{4. æ ·æœ¬å¤– \(R^2\)ï¼ˆOut-of-Sample

\section{åˆ†ç±»ä»»åŠ¡æŒ‡æ ‡}\label{ux5206ux7c7bux4efbux52a1ux6307ux6807}

\subsection{2. AUC-ROC
æ›²çº¿ä¸‹é¢ç§¯}\label{auc-roc-ux66f2ux7ebfux4e0bux9762ux79ef}

\textbf{ROC æ›²çº¿}ï¼šä¸åŒé˜ˆå€¼ä¸‹çš„çœŸæ­£ä¾‹çŽ‡ï¼ˆTPRï¼‰vs å‡æ­£ä¾‹çŽ‡ï¼ˆFPRï¼‰

\[

\textbf{AUC}ï¼ˆArea Under Curveï¼‰ï¼š

\begin{itemize}
\tightlist
\item
  èŒƒå›´ {[}0, 1{]}ï¼Œè¶Šå¤§è¶Šå¥½
\item
  0.5 è¡¨ç¤ºéšæœºçŒœæµ‹

  \textbf{è§£é‡Š}ï¼šéšæœºé€‰ä¸€å¯¹ï¼ˆæ­£ä¾‹ï¼Œè´Ÿä¾‹ï¼‰ï¼Œæ¨¡åž‹å¯¹æ­£ä¾‹æ‰“åˆ†æ›´é«˜çš„æ¦‚çŽ‡
\end{itemize}

\subsection{3. AUC-PRï¼ˆPrecision-Recall

\textbf{ç²¾ç¡®çŽ‡ä¸Žå¬å›žçŽ‡}ï¼š

\[

\]

\textbf{é€‚ç”¨åœºæ™¯}ï¼šç±»åˆ«æžä¸å¹³è¡¡æ—¶ï¼ˆå¦‚ä¿¡ç”¨è¿çº¦ã€æ¬ºè¯ˆæ£€æµ‹ï¼‰

\subsection{4. F1 åˆ†æ•°}\label{f1-ux5206ux6570}

\[

\]

\begin{itemize}
\tightlist
\item
  ç²¾ç¡®çŽ‡ä¸Žå¬å›žçŽ‡çš„è°ƒå’Œå¹³å‡
\item
  å•ä¸€é˜ˆå€¼ä¸‹çš„ç»¼åˆæŒ‡æ ‡
\end{itemize}

\subsection{5. æ ¡å‡†ï¼ˆCalibrationï¼‰}\label{ux6821ux51c6calibration}

\textbf{æ ¡å‡†å›¾}ï¼šå°†æ ·æœ¬æŒ‰ \(\hat{p}\) åˆ†æ¡¶ï¼Œæ£€æŸ¥æ¯æ¡¶å†…æ­£ä¾‹çš„çœŸå®žæ¯”ä¾‹ã€‚

\begin{tcolorbox}[enhanced jigsaw, bottomtitle=1mm, titlerule=0mm, arc=.35mm, colback=white, title=\textcolor{quarto-callout-tip-color}{\faLightbulb}\hspace{0.5em}{ðŸ’¡ æŒ‡æ ‡é€‰æ‹©çš„é»„é‡‘æ³•åˆ™}, coltitle=black, leftrule=.75mm, opacityback=0, colbacktitle=quarto-callout-tip-color!10!white, toprule=.15mm, opacitybacktitle=0.6, colframe=quarto-callout-tip-color-frame, toptitle=1mm, rightrule=.15mm, breakable, left=2mm, bottomrule=.15mm]

\section{ç±»åˆ«ä¸å¹³è¡¡çš„å¸¸è§è¯¯åŒº}\label{ux7c7bux522bux4e0dux5e73ux8861ux7684ux5e38ux89c1ux8befux533a}

\begin{Highlighting}[]

\subsection{ä¼ªä»£ç }\label{ux4f2aux4ee3ux7801}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{test\_scores }\OperatorTok{=}\NormalTok{ []}

\ControlFlowTok{for}\NormalTok{ test\_start }\KeywordTok{in}\NormalTok{ test\_periods:}
    \CommentTok{\# å¤–å±‚ï¼šå®šä¹‰æœ¬æœŸæµ‹è¯•é›†}
\NormalTok{    train\_val }\OperatorTok{=}\NormalTok{ data[data.date }\OperatorTok{\textless{}}\NormalTok{ test\_start]}
\NormalTok{    test }\OperatorTok{=}\NormalTok{ data[data.date }\OperatorTok{\textgreater{}=}\NormalTok{ test\_start]}
    
    \CommentTok{\# å†…å±‚ï¼šåœ¨ train\_val ä¸Šç”¨æ—¶åº CV é€‰è¶…å‚æ•°}
\NormalTok{    best\_lambda }\OperatorTok{=} \VariableTok{None}
\NormalTok{    best\_val\_score }\OperatorTok{=} \OperatorTok{{-}}\NormalTok{inf}
    
    \ControlFlowTok{for}\NormalTok{ lambda\_candidate }\KeywordTok{in}\NormalTok{ lambda\_grid:}
\NormalTok{        val\_scores\_inner }\OperatorTok{=}\NormalTok{ []}
        \ControlFlowTok{for}\NormalTok{ val\_start }\KeywordTok{in}\NormalTok{ validation\_periods:}
\NormalTok{            train\_inner }\OperatorTok{=}\NormalTok{ train\_val[train\_val.date }\OperatorTok{\textless{}}\NormalTok{ val\_start]}
\NormalTok{            val\_inner }\OperatorTok{=}\NormalTok{ train\_val[train\_val.date }\OperatorTok{\textgreater{}=}\NormalTok{ val\_start]}
            
\NormalTok{            model.fit(train\_inner, }\KeywordTok{lambda}\OperatorTok{=}\NormalTok{lambda\_candidate)}
\NormalTok{            val\_scores\_inner.append(model.score(val\_inner))}
        
\NormalTok{        avg\_val\_score }\OperatorTok{=}\NormalTok{ mean(val\_scores\_inner)}
        \ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ avg\_val\_score }\OperatorTok{\textgreater{}}\NormalTok{ best\_val\_score:}
\NormalTok{            best\_val\_score }\OperatorTok{=}\NormalTok{ avg\_val\_score}
\NormalTok{            best\_lambda }\OperatorTok{=}\NormalTok{ lambda\_candidate}
    
    \CommentTok{\# å¤–å±‚ï¼šç”¨æœ€ä¼˜è¶…å‚æ•°è®­ç»ƒæœ€ç»ˆæ¨¡åž‹}
\NormalTok{    model.fit(train\_val, }\KeywordTok{lambda}\OperatorTok{=}\NormalTok{best\_lambda)}
\NormalTok{    test\_scores.append(model.score(test))}

\CommentTok{\# æŠ¥å‘Šæ ·æœ¬å¤–æ€§èƒ½}
\NormalTok{final\_oos\_score }\OperatorTok{=}\NormalTok{ mean(test\_scores)}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\section{é¢„æµ‹å±‚é¢æŒ‡æ ‡}\label{ux9884ux6d4bux5c42ux9762ux6307ux6807}

\subsection{\texorpdfstring{1. æ ·æœ¬å¤– \(R^2\)ï¼ˆOut-of-Sample
\(R^2\)ï¼‰}{1. æ ·æœ¬å¤– R\^{}2ï¼ˆOut-of-Sample R\^{}2ï¼‰}}\label{ux6837ux672cux5916-r2out-of-sample-r2-1}

\[

å…¶ä¸­ \(\bar{r}_{\text{hist}}\) æ˜¯åŽ†å²å‡å€¼ï¼ˆä»…ç”¨è®­ç»ƒæœŸï¼‰ã€‚

\textbf{è§£é‡Š}ï¼š

\begin{itemize}

\item
  ç›¸å¯¹äºŽ''åŽ†å²å‡å€¼é¢„æµ‹''çš„æ”¹è¿›
\item
  å¯èƒ½ä¸ºè´Ÿï¼ˆæ¨¡åž‹æ¯”å‡å€¼è¿˜å·®ï¼‰
\item
  GKY (2020) ä¸­ \(R^2_{\text{OOS}} \approx 0.5\%\) å·²å±žä¼˜ç§€
\end{itemize}

\subsection{2. ä¿¡æ¯ç³»æ•°ï¼ˆICï¼‰ä¸Ž Rank
IC}\label{ux4fe1ux606fux7cfbux6570icux4e0e-rank-ic}

\textbf{IC}ï¼ˆInformation Coefficientï¼‰ï¼šé¢„æµ‹å€¼ä¸Žå®žé™…å€¼çš„ç›¸å…³ç³»æ•°

\[

\]

\textbf{Rank IC}ï¼šæŽ’åºç›¸å…³ï¼ˆSpearmanï¼‰

\[

\]

\textbf{ä¼˜ç‚¹}ï¼š

\begin{itemize}
\tightlist
\item
  æ›´å…³æ³¨æŽ’åºè€Œéžæ•°å€¼ç²¾åº¦
\item
  å¯¹å¼‚å¸¸å€¼æ›´é²æ£’ï¼ˆRank ICï¼‰
\end{itemize}

\textbf{å…¸åž‹å€¼}ï¼š

\begin{itemize}
\tightlist
\item
  \(|\text{IC}| > 0.05\) å·²æœ‰å®žç”¨ä»·å€¼
\item
  \(|\text{IC}| > 0.10\) å±žå¼ºä¿¡å·
\end{itemize}

\section{ç»„åˆå±‚é¢æŒ‡æ ‡}\label{ux7ec4ux5408ux5c42ux9762ux6307ux6807}

\subsection{1. å¹´åŒ–è¶…é¢æ”¶ç›Š}\label{ux5e74ux5316ux8d85ux989dux6536ux76ca}

\textbf{è§£é‡Š}ï¼šå•ä½é£Žé™©çš„è¶…é¢æ”¶ç›Š

\subsection{3. ä¿¡æ¯æ¯”çŽ‡ï¼ˆInformation

\textbf{è§£é‡Š}ï¼šç›¸å¯¹åŸºå‡†çš„è¶…é¢æ”¶ç›Šç¨³å®šæ€§

\subsection{4. æœ€å¤§å›žæ’¤ï¼ˆMaximum

\textbf{è§£é‡Š}ï¼šä»Žå³°å€¼åˆ°è°·åº•çš„æœ€å¤§æŸå¤±

\subsection{5. æ¢æ‰‹çŽ‡ï¼ˆTurnoverï¼‰}\label{ux6362ux624bux7387turnover}

\[

å…¶ä¸­ \(w_{i,t-1}^+\) æ˜¯ \(t-1\) æœŸæœ«æŒä»“æƒé‡ï¼ˆè€ƒè™‘ä»·æ ¼å˜åŒ–ï¼‰ã€‚

\subsection{1.

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{\# æ¯æœŸæŒ‰é¢„æµ‹åˆ†æ•°æŽ’åº}

\CommentTok{\# æž„å»ºå¤šç©ºç»„åˆ}

\subsection{2. è¯å…¸æ³•ï¼ˆDictionary-based

\textbf{æ€æƒ³}ï¼šç”¨\textbf{é¢„å®šä¹‰è¯è¡¨}åŒ¹é…æ–‡æœ¬ï¼Œè®¡ç®—æƒ…æ„Ÿ/ä¸»é¢˜å¾—åˆ†ã€‚

\textbf{ç»å…¸è¯å…¸}ï¼š

  \begin{itemize}

  \item

\item

\textbf{è®¡ç®—}ï¼š

\[
\text{Sentiment Score} = \frac{\#\text{Positive Words} - \#\text{Negative Words}}{\#\text{Total Words}}
\]

\textbf{é‡‘èžåº”ç”¨æ¡ˆä¾‹}ï¼š

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{\# å¹´æŠ¥æ–‡æœ¬æƒ…æ„Ÿåˆ†æž}
\NormalTok{positive\_words }\OperatorTok{=}\NormalTok{ \{}\StringTok{\textquotesingle{}growth\textquotesingle{}}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{\textquotesingle{}profit\textquotesingle{}}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{\textquotesingle{}opportunity\textquotesingle{}}\NormalTok{, ...\}}
\NormalTok{negative\_words }\OperatorTok{=}\NormalTok{ \{}\StringTok{\textquotesingle{}loss\textquotesingle{}}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{\textquotesingle{}risk\textquotesingle{}}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{\textquotesingle{}decline\textquotesingle{}}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{\textquotesingle{}uncertainty\textquotesingle{}}\NormalTok{, ...\}}

\KeywordTok{def}\NormalTok{ sentiment(text):}
\NormalTok{    tokens }\OperatorTok{=}\NormalTok{ tokenize(text.lower())}
\NormalTok{    pos }\OperatorTok{=} \BuiltInTok{sum}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{1} \ControlFlowTok{for}\NormalTok{ w }\KeywordTok{in}\NormalTok{ tokens }\ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ w }\KeywordTok{in}\NormalTok{ positive\_words)}
\NormalTok{    neg }\OperatorTok{=} \BuiltInTok{sum}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{1} \ControlFlowTok{for}\NormalTok{ w }\KeywordTok{in}\NormalTok{ tokens }\ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ w }\KeywordTok{in}\NormalTok{ negative\_words)}
    \ControlFlowTok{return}\NormalTok{ (pos }\OperatorTok{{-}}\NormalTok{ neg) }\OperatorTok{/} \BuiltInTok{len}\NormalTok{(tokens)}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\textbf{ä¼˜ç‚¹}ï¼š

\begin{itemize}
\tightlist
\item
  é«˜åº¦å¯è§£é‡Šï¼ˆå¯è¿½æº¯åˆ°å…·ä½“è¯ï¼‰
\item
  ç¨³å®šï¼ˆä¸éœ€è®­ç»ƒï¼‰
\item
  é€‚åˆç›‘ç®¡å®¡è®¡
\end{itemize}

  å¿½ç•¥ä¸Šä¸‹æ–‡ï¼ˆ``not good'' è¢«è¯¯åˆ¤ä¸ºæ­£é¢ï¼‰

\subsection{5. Transformer ä¸Ž BERT}\label{transformer-ux4e0e-bert}

\textbf{é©å‘½æ€§çªç ´}ï¼š\textbf{ä¸Šä¸‹æ–‡åŒ–åµŒå…¥}ï¼ˆContextualized Embeddingsï¼‰

\textbf{BERTï¼ˆBidirectional Encoder Representations from Transformersï¼‰}

\begin{itemize}
\tightlist
\item
  Devlin et al.~(2019)
\end{itemize}

\textbf{æ ¸å¿ƒæ€æƒ³}ï¼š

\begin{itemize}
\tightlist
\item
  åŒä¸€ä¸ªè¯åœ¨ä¸åŒä¸Šä¸‹æ–‡ä¸­æœ‰\textbf{ä¸åŒçš„å‘é‡}
\item
  åŒå‘æ³¨æ„åŠ›æœºåˆ¶ï¼ˆTransformerï¼‰
\end{itemize}

\textbf{ç¤ºä¾‹}ï¼š

\begin{verbatim}
å¥1: "I went to the bank to deposit money."
     â†’ "bank" å‘é‡åå‘"é‡‘èžæœºæž„"

å¥2: "I sat by the river bank."
     â†’ "bank" å‘é‡åå‘"æ²³å²¸"
\end{verbatim}

\textbf{é¢„è®­ç»ƒä»»åŠ¡}ï¼š

\begin{enumerate}
\def\labelenumi{\arabic{enumi}.}
\item
  \textbf{Masked Language Modeling (MLM)}ï¼š

\begin{verbatim}
è¾“å…¥: "The company's [MASK] grew by 15%."
é¢„æµ‹: revenue / profit / sales
\end{verbatim}
\item
  \textbf{Next Sentence Prediction (NSP)}ï¼š

\begin{verbatim}
å¥A: "Revenue increased."
å¥B: "Profit margins improved."
é¢„æµ‹: B æ˜¯å¦æ˜¯ A çš„ä¸‹ä¸€å¥ï¼Ÿ
\end{verbatim}
\end{enumerate}

\textbf{é‡‘èžé¢†åŸŸé¢„è®­ç»ƒæ¨¡åž‹}ï¼š

\begin{itemize}
\tightlist
\item
  \textbf{FinBERT} (Araci, 2019)ï¼šåœ¨é‡‘èžæ–°é—»/å¹´æŠ¥ä¸Šå¾®è°ƒ
\item
  \textbf{DistilRoBERTa-financial-sentiment}ï¼šè½»é‡çº§é‡‘èžæƒ…æ„Ÿåˆ†ç±»
\end{itemize}

\textbf{ä½¿ç”¨æµç¨‹}ï¼š

\begin{Shaded}

\subsection{æå–ç¤ºä¾‹ï¼šéŸµå¾‹ç‰¹å¾}\label{ux63d0ux53d6ux793aux4f8bux97f5ux5f8bux7279ux5f81}

\ImportTok{import}\NormalTok{ numpy }\ImportTok{as}\NormalTok{ np}

\CommentTok{\# åŠ è½½éŸ³é¢‘}

    \KeywordTok{def} \FunctionTok{\_\_init\_\_}\NormalTok{(}\VariableTok{self}\NormalTok{, input\_dim}\OperatorTok{=}\DecValTok{2048}\NormalTok{, hidden\_dim}\OperatorTok{=}\DecValTok{512}\NormalTok{, num\_classes}\OperatorTok{=}\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{):}
        \BuiltInTok{super}\NormalTok{().}\FunctionTok{\_\_init\_\_}\NormalTok{()}
        \VariableTok{self}\NormalTok{.lstm }\OperatorTok{=}\NormalTok{ nn.LSTM(input\_dim, hidden\_dim, batch\_first}\OperatorTok{=}\VariableTok{True}\NormalTok{)}
        \VariableTok{self}\NormalTok{.fc }\OperatorTok{=}\NormalTok{ nn.Linear(hidden\_dim, num\_classes)}
    
    \KeywordTok{def}\NormalTok{ forward(}\VariableTok{self}\NormalTok{, x):}
        \CommentTok{\# x: (batch, seq\_len, input\_dim)}
\NormalTok{        \_, (h\_n, \_) }\OperatorTok{=} \VariableTok{self}\NormalTok{.lstm(x)}
        \CommentTok{\# h\_n: (1, batch, hidden\_dim)}
\NormalTok{        out }\OperatorTok{=} \VariableTok{self}\NormalTok{.fc(h\_n.squeeze(}\DecValTok{0}\NormalTok{))}
        \ControlFlowTok{return}\NormalTok{ out}

\CommentTok{\# è®­ç»ƒ}
\NormalTok{model }\OperatorTok{=}\NormalTok{ VideoClassifier()}
\NormalTok{optimizer }\OperatorTok{=}\NormalTok{ torch.optim.Adam(model.parameters())}
\NormalTok{criterion }\OperatorTok{=}\NormalTok{ nn.CrossEntropyLoss()}

\ControlFlowTok{for}\NormalTok{ epoch }\KeywordTok{in} \BuiltInTok{range}\NormalTok{(num\_epochs):}
    \ControlFlowTok{for}\NormalTok{ video\_features, labels }\KeywordTok{in}\NormalTok{ dataloader:}
\NormalTok{        optimizer.zero\_grad()}
\NormalTok{        outputs }\OperatorTok{=}\NormalTok{ model(video\_features)}
\NormalTok{        loss }\OperatorTok{=}\NormalTok{ criterion(outputs, labels)}
\NormalTok{        loss.backward()}
\NormalTok{        optimizer.step()}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\KeywordTok{class}\NormalTok{ MidFusionModel(nn.Module):}
    \KeywordTok{def} \FunctionTok{\_\_init\_\_}\NormalTok{(}\VariableTok{self}\NormalTok{):}
        \BuiltInTok{super}\NormalTok{().}\FunctionTok{\_\_init\_\_}\NormalTok{()}
        \VariableTok{self}\NormalTok{.image\_encoder }\OperatorTok{=}\NormalTok{ nn.Linear(}\DecValTok{2048}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{512}\NormalTok{)}
        \VariableTok{self}\NormalTok{.audio\_encoder }\OperatorTok{=}\NormalTok{ nn.Linear(}\DecValTok{768}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{512}\NormalTok{)}
        \VariableTok{self}\NormalTok{.text\_encoder }\OperatorTok{=}\NormalTok{ nn.Linear(}\DecValTok{768}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{512}\NormalTok{)}
        \VariableTok{self}\NormalTok{.fusion }\OperatorTok{=}\NormalTok{ nn.Linear(}\DecValTok{512}\OperatorTok{*}\DecValTok{3}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{256}\NormalTok{)}
        \VariableTok{self}\NormalTok{.classifier }\OperatorTok{=}\NormalTok{ nn.Linear(}\DecValTok{256}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{)}
    
    \KeywordTok{def}\NormalTok{ forward(}\VariableTok{self}\NormalTok{, image, audio, text):}

\NormalTok{        aud\_emb }\OperatorTok{=} \VariableTok{self}\NormalTok{.audio\_encoder(audio)}

        \ControlFlowTok{return} \VariableTok{self}\NormalTok{.classifier(fused)}

\subsection{4.
æ³¨æ„åŠ›èžåˆï¼ˆAttention-basedï¼‰}\label{ux6ce8ux610fux529bux878dux5408attention-based}

\textbf{è‡ªåŠ¨å­¦ä¹ å„æ¨¡æ€çš„æƒé‡}ï¼š

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\KeywordTok{class}\NormalTok{ AttentionFusion(nn.Module):}
    \KeywordTok{def} \FunctionTok{\_\_init\_\_}\NormalTok{(}\VariableTok{self}\NormalTok{, input\_dim}\OperatorTok{=}\DecValTok{512}\NormalTok{):}
        \BuiltInTok{super}\NormalTok{().}\FunctionTok{\_\_init\_\_}\NormalTok{()}
        \VariableTok{self}\NormalTok{.attention }\OperatorTok{=}\NormalTok{ nn.Linear(input\_dim, }\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{)}
    
    \KeywordTok{def}\NormalTok{ forward(}\VariableTok{self}\NormalTok{, modalities):}
        \CommentTok{\# modalities: list of (batch, input\_dim)}
\NormalTok{        stacked }\OperatorTok{=}\NormalTok{ torch.stack(modalities, dim}\OperatorTok{=}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{)  }\CommentTok{\# (batch, n\_modalities, input\_dim)}
        
        \CommentTok{\# è®¡ç®—æ³¨æ„åŠ›æƒé‡}

        \CommentTok{\# åŠ æƒå’Œ}
\NormalTok{        fused }\OperatorTok{=}\NormalTok{ (stacked }\OperatorTok{*}\NormalTok{ attn\_weights).}\BuiltInTok{sum}\NormalTok{(dim}\OperatorTok{=}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{)  }\CommentTok{\# (batch, input\_dim)}
        \ControlFlowTok{return}\NormalTok{ fused}
\end{Highlighting}
